	<div id='readme' style='width:70%;margin-left:25%;'>
	   	<article class='markdown-body'>
		<html>
 <head></head>
 <body>
  <h1><a href="#k8s集群安装" name="k8s集群安装">K8S集群安装</a></h1> 
  <h1><a href="#一-环境准备" name="一-环境准备">一、 环境准备</a></h1> 
  <h2>1. 1 机器环境</h2> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p><font color="red">非常重要必须看咯</font></p> 
   <p>1、节点CPU核数必须是 ：&gt;= 2核 /内存要求必须是：&gt;=2G ，否则k8s无法启动</p> 
   <p>2、DNS网络： 最好设置为 本地网络连通的DNS,否则网络不通，无法下载一些镜像</p> 
   <p>3、兼容问题</p> 
   <p>docker 19 kubernetes1.19.x</p> 
   <p>docker 20 kubernetes 1.20.x</p> 
   <p>在k8s1.21.1之后 k8s的默认容器不是Docker是Containerd （需要的 可以找我拿公开课）</p> 
   <p><strong>注意：</strong>使用docker版本v20.10.10、kubernetes v1.23.0、Go版本v1.13.15</p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <table> 
   <thead> 
    <tr> 
     <th>节点hostname </th> 
     <th>作用 </th> 
     <th>IP </th> 
    </tr> 
   </thead> 
   <tbody> 
    <tr> 
     <td>master </td> 
     <td>master </td> 
     <td>192.168.3.221 </td> 
    </tr> 
    <tr> 
     <td>worker1 </td> 
     <td>work1 </td> 
     <td>192.168.3.222 </td> 
    </tr> 
    <tr> 
     <td>worker2 </td> 
     <td>work2 </td> 
     <td>192.168.3.223 </td> 
    </tr> 
   </tbody> 
  </table> 
  <h2>1.2 设置主机别名</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">[root@localhost ~]# hostnamectl set-hostname master --static
[root@localhost ~]# hostnamectl set-hostname worker1 --static
[root@localhost ~]# hostnamectl set-hostname worker2 --static
</code></pre> 
  <h2>1.3 服务器静态IP配置</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">[root@localhost ~]# vi /etc/sysconfig/network-scripts/ifcfg-enp0s3
BOOTPROTO="static" #dhcp改为static 
ONBOOT="yes" #开机启用本配置
IPADDR=192.168.3.10 #静态IP 192.168.8.11/192.168.8.12
GATEWAY=192.168.3.1 #默认网关
NETMASK=255.255.255.0 #子网掩码
DNS1=114.114.114.114 #DNS 配置
DNS2=8.8.8.8 #DNS 配置【必须配置，否则SDK镜像下载很慢】

## 重启所有服务器
[root@localhost ~] reboot 
</code></pre> 
  <h2>1.4 查看主机名</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">## 看看别名是否生效
hostname
</code></pre> 
  <h2>1.5 配置IP host映射关系</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">## 编辑/etc/hosts文件，配置映射关系
vi /etc/hosts
192.168.3.10 kmaster
192.168.3.11 kworker1
192.168.3.12 kworker2
</code></pre> 
  <h2>1.6 安装依赖环境</h2> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p><font color="red">注意：每一台机器都需要安装此依赖环境</font></p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <pre><code class="bash">yum install -y conntrack ntpdate ntp ipvsadm ipset jq iptables curl sysstatlibseccomp wget vim net-tools git iproute lrzsz bash-completion tree bridge-utils unzip bind-utils gcc
</code></pre> 
  <h2>1.7 防火墙配置</h2> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p>安装iptables，启动iptables，设置开机自启，清空iptables规则，保存当前规则到默认规则</p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <pre><code class="bash"># 关闭防火墙(生产环境建议使用放行端口)
systemctl stop firewalld &amp;&amp; systemctl disable firewalld
# 置空iptables （生产环境别执行）
yum -y install iptables-services &amp;&amp; systemctl start iptables &amp;&amp; systemctl enable iptables &amp;&amp; iptables -F &amp;&amp; service iptables save
</code></pre> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p>如果是在服务上部署必须放开下面端口(包括tcp/6443[tcp/udp])<br><img alt="image-20211213203239378"></p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <h2>1.8 关闭selinux[必须操作]</h2> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p>因为在K8S集群安装的时候需要执行脚本，如果Selinux没有关闭它会阻止执行。</p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <pre><code class="bash"># 关闭swap分区【虚拟内存】并且永久关闭虚拟内存
swapoff -a &amp;&amp; sed -i '/ swap / s/^\(.*\)$/#\1/g' /etc/fstab
# 关闭selinux
setenforce 0 &amp;&amp; sed -i 's/^SELINUX=.*/SELINUX=disabled/' /etc/selinux/config
</code></pre> 
  <h1><a href="#二-系统设置调整" name="二-系统设置调整">二、系统设置调整</a></h1> 
  <h2>2.1 调整内核参数</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">cat &gt; kubernetes.conf &lt;&lt;EOF
net.bridge.bridge-nf-call-iptables=1
net.bridge.bridge-nf-call-ip6tables=1
net.ipv4.ip_forward=1
net.ipv4.tcp_tw_recycle=0
vm.swappiness=0
vm.overcommit_memory=1
vm.panic_on_oom=0
fs.inotify.max_user_instances=8192
fs.inotify.max_user_watches=1048576
fs.file-max=52706963
fs.nr_open=52706963
net.ipv6.conf.all.disable_ipv6=1
net.netfilter.nf_conntrack_max=2310720
EOF

#将优化内核文件拷贝到/etc/sysctl.d/文件夹下，这样优化文件开机的时候能够被调用
cp kubernetes.conf /etc/sysctl.d/kubernetes.conf
#手动刷新，让优化文件立即生效
sysctl -p /etc/sysctl.d/kubernetes.conf
</code></pre> 
  <h2>2.2 调整系统临时区</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">#设置系统时区为中国/上海
timedatectl set-timezone "Asia/Shanghai"
#将当前的UTC 时间写入硬件时钟
timedatectl set-local-rtc 0
#重启依赖于系统时间的服务
systemctl restart rsyslog
systemctl restart crond
</code></pre> 
  <h2>2.3 升级内存为5.4</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">## 查看内核 (3.10的内核对于新版本不太稳定)
uname -r
3.10.xxx 建议升级到5.4.164-1.el7.elrepo.x86_64 
## 升级内核
rpm -Uvh http://www.elrepo.org/elrepo-release-7.0-3.el7.elrepo.noarch.rpm
yum --enablerepo=elrepo-kernel install -y kernel-lt
grub2-set-default 'CentOS Linux (5.4.159-1.el7.elrepo.x86_64) 7 (Core)'
reboot
</code></pre> 
  <h2>2.4 设置日志保存方式</h2> 
  <h3>2.4.1 创建保存日志的目录</h3> 
  <pre><code class="bash">mkdir /var/log/journal
</code></pre> 
  <h3>2.4.2 创建配置文件存放目录</h3> 
  <pre><code class="bash">mkdir /etc/systemd/journald.conf.d
</code></pre> 
  <h3>2.4.3 创建配置文件</h3> 
  <pre><code class="bash">cat &gt; /etc/systemd/journald.conf.d/99-prophet.conf &lt;&lt;EOF
[Journal]
Storage=persistent
Compress=yes
SyncIntervalSec=5m
RateLimitInterval=30s
RateLimitBurst=1000
SystemMaxUse=10G
SystemMaxFileSize=200M
MaxRetentionSec=2week
ForwardToSyslog=no
EOF
</code></pre> 
  <h3>2.4.4 重启systemd journald 的配置</h3> 
  <pre><code class="bash">systemctl restart systemd-journald
</code></pre> 
  <h3>2.4.5 打开文件数调整(可忽略，不执行)</h3> 
  <pre><code class="bash">echo "* soft nofile 65536" &gt;&gt; /etc/security/limits.conf
echo "* hard nofile 65536" &gt;&gt; /etc/security/limits.conf
</code></pre> 
  <h3>2.4.6 kube-proxy 开启 ipvs 前置条件</h3> 
  <pre><code class="bash">modprobe br_netfilter
cat &gt; /etc/sysconfig/modules/ipvs.modules &lt;&lt;EOF
#!/bin/bash
modprobe -- ip_vs
modprobe -- ip_vs_rr
modprobe -- ip_vs_wrr
modprobe -- ip_vs_sh
modprobe -- nf_conntrack
EOF
#使用lsmod命令查看这些文件是否被引导
chmod 755 /etc/sysconfig/modules/ipvs.modules &amp;&amp; bash /etc/sysconfig/modules/ipvs.modules &amp;&amp; lsmod | grep -e ip_vs -e nf_conntrack
=========================执行结果================================
nf_conntrack_netlink    45056  0 
nfnetlink              16384  4 nf_conntrack_netlink,nf_tables,ip_set
ip_vs_sh               16384  0 
ip_vs_wrr              16384  0 
ip_vs_rr               16384  4 
ip_vs                 155648  10 ip_vs_rr,ip_vs_sh,ip_vs_wrr
nf_conntrack          147456  6 xt_conntrack,nf_nat,xt_nat,nf_conntrack_netlink,xt_MASQUERADE,ip_vs
nf_defrag_ipv6         24576  2 nf_conntrack,ip_vs
nf_defrag_ipv4         16384  1 nf_conntrack
libcrc32c              16384  4 nf_conntrack,nf_nat,xfs,ip_vs
</code></pre> 
  <h1><a href="#三-docker部署" name="三-docker部署">三、Docker部署</a></h1> 
  <h2>3.1 安装docker</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash"># 安装依赖
yum install -y yum-utils device-mapper-persistent-data lvm2
#紧接着配置一个稳定的仓库、仓库配置会保存到/etc/yum.repos.d/docker-ce.repo文件中
yum-config-manager --add-repo https://download.docker.com/linux/centos/docker-ce.repo
#更新Yum安装的相关Docker软件包&amp;安装Docker CE(这里安装Docker最新版本)
yum update -y &amp;&amp; yum install docker-ce
</code></pre> 
  <h2>3.2 设置docker daemon文件</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">#创建/etc/docker目录
mkdir /etc/docker
#更新daemon.json文件
cat &gt; /etc/docker/daemon.json &lt;&lt;EOF
{
  "registry-mirrors": [
        "https://ebkn7ykm.mirror.aliyuncs.com",
        "https://docker.mirrors.ustc.edu.cn",
        "http://f1361db2.m.daocloud.io",
        "https://registry.docker-cn.com"
    ],
  "exec-opts": ["native.cgroupdriver=systemd"],
  "log-driver": "json-file",
  "log-opts": {
    "max-size": "100m"
  },
  "storage-driver": "overlay2"
}
EOF
#注意：一定注意编码问题，出现错误---查看命令：journalctl -amu docker 即可发现错误
#创建，存储docker配置文件
# mkdir -p /etc/systemd/system/docker.service.d
</code></pre> 
  <h2>3.3 重启docker服务</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash">systemctl daemon-reload &amp;&amp; systemctl restart docker &amp;&amp; systemctl enable docker
</code></pre> 
  <h1><a href="#四-kubeadm安装k8s" name="四-kubeadm安装k8s">四、kubeadm安装K8S</a></h1> 
  <h2>4.1 yum仓库镜像</h2> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p>国内镜像配置(国内建议配置)</p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <pre><code class="bash">cat &lt;&lt;EOF &gt; /etc/yum.repos.d/kubernetes.repo
[kubernetes]
name=Kubernetes
baseurl=http://mirrors.aliyun.com/kubernetes/yum/repos/kubernetes-el7-x86_64
enabled=1
gpgcheck=0
repo_gpgcheck=0
gpgkey=http://mirrors.aliyun.com/kubernetes/yum/doc/yum-key.gpg
       http://mirrors.aliyun.com/kubernetes/yum/doc/rpm-package-key.gpg
EOF
</code></pre> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p>官网镜像配置</p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <pre><code class="bash">cat &lt;&lt;EOF &gt; /etc/yum.repos.d/kubernetes.repo
[kubernetes]
name=Kubernetes
baseurl=https://packages.cloud.google.com/yum/repos/kubernetes-el7-x86_64
enabled=1
gpgcheck=1
repo_gpgcheck=1
gpgkey=https://packages.cloud.google.com/yum/doc/yum-key.gpg https://packages.cloud.google.com/yum/doc/rpm-package-key.gpg
EOF
</code></pre> 
  <h2>4.2 安装kubeadm 、kubelet、kubectl(1.23.0)</h2> 
  <pre><code class="bash"># 指定版本
yum install -y kubelet-1.23.0 kubeadm-1.23.0 kubectl-1.23.0 --disableexcludes=kubernetes
systemctl enable kubelet &amp;&amp; systemctl start kubelet
</code></pre> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p>注意：以上操作所有机器都必须安装</p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <h1><a href="#五-准备k8s镜像" name="五-准备k8s镜像">五、准备k8s镜像</a></h1> 
  <h2>5.1 修改配置文件</h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">[root@master ~]$ kubeadm config print init-defaults &gt; kubeadm-init.yaml
</code></pre> 
  <p>该文件有两处需要修改:</p> 
  <ul> 
   <li>将<code>advertiseAddress: 1.2.3.4</code>修改为本机地址,比如使用192.168.3.191作为master，就修改<code>advertiseAddress: 192.168.3.191</code></li> 
   <li>将<code>imageRepository: k8s.gcr.io</code>修改为<code>imageRepository: registry.cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/google_containers</code></li> 
  </ul> 
  <p>修改完毕后文件如下:</p> 
  <pre><code class="yaml">apiVersion: kubeadm.k8s.io/v1beta2
bootstrapTokens:
- groups:
  - system:bootstrappers:kubeadm:default-node-token
  token: abcdef.0123456789abcdef
  ttl: 24h0m0s
  usages:
  - signing
  - authentication
kind: InitConfiguration
localAPIEndpoint:
  advertiseAddress: 192.168.3.191 # 本机IP
  bindPort: 6443
nodeRegistration:
  criSocket: /var/run/dockershim.sock
  name: k8s-master
  taints:
  - effect: NoSchedule
    key: node-role.kubernetes.io/master
---
apiServer:
  timeoutForControlPlane: 4m0s
apiVersion: kubeadm.k8s.io/v1beta2
certificatesDir: /etc/kubernetes/pki
clusterName: kubernetes
controllerManager: {}
dns:
  type: CoreDNS
etcd:
  local:
    dataDir: /var/lib/etcd
imageRepository: registry.cn-hangzhou.aliyuncs.com/google_containers #镜像仓库
kind: ClusterConfiguration
kubernetesVersion: v1.20.1
networking:
  dnsDomain: cluster.local
  serviceSubnet: 10.96.0.0/12
  podSubnet: 10.244.0.0/16 # 新增Pod子网络
scheduler: {}
</code></pre> 
  <h2>5.2 根据配置文件拉取镜像</h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">[root@kmaster ~]$ kubeadm config images pull --config kubeadm-init.yaml
</code></pre> 
  <h1><a href="#六-k8s的master部署" name="六-k8s的master部署">六、K8S的Master部署</a></h1> 
  <h2>6.1 执行初始化</h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">[root@master ~]$ kubeadm init --config kubeadm-init.yaml
</code></pre> 
  <h2>6.2 验证是否成功</h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">## 如果在执行完成后出现下面的语句 代表成功 并记录下加入worker节点的命令
kubeadm join 192.168.3.10:6443 --token abcdef.0123456789abcdef \
    --discovery-token-ca-cert-hash sha256:13aff92657d0f3451ac68e3200ebc3c1c6ea6980b1de700ba257ad1538e0ce3
</code></pre> 
  <h2>6.3 查看Master节点网络状态</h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">## 配置kubectl执行命令环境
mkdir -p $HOME/.kube
cp -i /etc/kubernetes/admin.conf $HOME/.kube/config
chown $(id -u):$(id -g) $HOME/.kube/config

## 执行kubectl命令查看机器节点
kubectl get node
-----------------------------------------
NAME     STATUS     ROLES    AGE   VERSION
master   NotReady   master   48m   v1.20.1

## 发现节点STATUS是NotReady的，是因为没有配置网络
</code></pre> 
  <h2>6.4 配置网络</h2> 
  <p>使用以下命令安装Calico网络</p> 
  <pre><code class="bash">wget https://docs.projectcalico.org/manifests/calico.yaml

## 编辑calico.yaml
## 修改calico.yaml文件设置指定的网卡
# Cluster type to identify the deployment type
- name: CLUSTER_TYPE
value: "k8s,bgp"
# IP automatic detection
- name: IP_AUTODETECTION_METHOD
value: "interface=en.*"
# Auto-detect the BGP IP address.
- name: IP
value: "autodetect"
# Enable IPIP
- name: CALICO_IPV4POOL_IPIP
value: "Never"
## 构建calico网络
kubectl apply -f calico.yaml
</code></pre> 
  <p>此时查看node信息, master的状态已经是<code>Ready</code>了.</p> 
  <pre><code class="yacas">[root@master ~]$ kubectl get node
NAME     STATUS     ROLES    AGE   VERSION
master   Ready   master   48m      v1.20.5
</code></pre> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p>看到STATUS是Ready的，说明网络已经通了。</p> 
  </blockquote> 
  <h1><a href="#七-追加node节点" name="七-追加node节点">七、追加Node节点</a></h1> 
  <pre><code class="bash">## 到其他几个node节点进行执行即可
kubeadm join 192.168.3.10:6443 --token abcdef.0123456789abcdef \
    --discovery-token-ca-cert-hash sha256:37eb59b3459a1651222a98e35d057cfd102e8ae311c5fc9bb4be22cd46a59c29
</code></pre> 
  <h1><a href="#八-验证状态" name="八-验证状态">八、验证状态</a></h1> 
  <pre><code class="bash">[root@kmaster ~]# kubectl get node
NAME      STATUS   ROLES                  AGE     VERSION
kmaster   Ready    control-plane,master   26m     v1.20.5
kworker1    Ready    &lt;none&gt;                 5m37s   v1.20.5
kworker2    Ready    &lt;none&gt;                 5m28s   v1.20.5

[root@kmaster ~]# kubectl get pod -n kube-system -o wide
## 如果看到下面的pod状态都是Running状态，说明K8S集群环境就构建完成
</code></pre> 
  <h1><a href="#安装-kubernetes-dashboard" name="安装-kubernetes-dashboard">安装 Kubernetes Dashboard</a></h1> 
  <h2><a href="#下载dashboard" name="下载dashboard">下载Dashboard</a></h2> 
  <p><a href="https://github.com/kubernetes/dashboard/releases">下载Dashboard</a></p> 
  <h2><a href="#安装" name="安装">安装</a></h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">kubectl apply -f https://raw.githubusercontent.com/kubernetes/dashboard/v2.4.0/aio/deploy/recommended.yaml
</code></pre> 
  <h2>创建dashboard-admin.yaml</h2> 
  <pre><code class="yaml">cat &gt; dashboard-admin.yaml &lt;&lt; EOF
kind: ClusterRoleBinding
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1
metadata:
  name: admin
  annotations:
    rbac.authorization.kubernetes.io/autoupdate: "true"
roleRef:
  kind: ClusterRole
  name: cluster-admin
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io
subjects:
- kind: ServiceAccount
  name: admin
  namespace: kube-system
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: ServiceAccount
metadata:
  name: admin
  namespace: kube-system
  labels:
    kubernetes.io/cluster-service: "true"
    addonmanager.kubernetes.io/mode: Reconcile
EOF
</code></pre> 
  <h2><a href="#创建登录用户" name="创建登录用户">创建登录用户</a></h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">kubectl apply -f dashboard-admin.yaml
</code></pre> 
  <h2>查看admin-user账户的token</h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">kubectl -n kube-system get secret|grep admin-token

kubectl -n kube-system describe secret admin-token-w94tz

## 直接获取token
kubectl -n kube-system get secret admin-token-w94tz -o jsonpath={.data.token}|base64 -d
</code></pre> 
  <h2><a href="#火狐浏览器直接访问-输入token即可正常访问" name="火狐浏览器直接访问-输入token即可正常访问">火狐浏览器直接访问，输入token即可正常访问</a></h2> 
  <pre><code class="shell">https://192.168.3.251:31443/
</code></pre> 
  <blockquote> 
   <p>解决谷歌无法验证证书问题</p> 
   <pre><code class="shell">openssl genrsa -out dashboard.key 2048
# 172.16.64.229为master节点的IP地址
openssl req -new -out dashboard.csr -key dashboard.key -subj '/CN=172.16.64.229'
openssl x509 -req -in dashboard.csr -signkey dashboard.key -out dashboard.crt

kubectl delete secret kubernetes-dashboard-certs -n kubernetes-dashboard

kubectl create secret generic kubernetes-dashboard-certs --from-file=dashboard.key --from-file=dashboard.crt -n kubernetes-dashboard

kubectl get pod -n kubernetes-dashboard

kubectl delete po kubernetes-dashboard-b65488c4-rcdjh -n kubernetes-dashboard
## 批量删除
kubectl get pod -n kubernetes-dashboard | grep -v NAME | awk '{print "kubectl delete po " $1 " -n kubernetes-dashboard"}' | sh

</code></pre> 
   <pre><code class="shell">kubectl apply -f https://raw.githubusercontent.com/kubernetes/dashboard/v2.0.5/aio/deploy/recommended.yaml

所以我们找到配置文件：https://github.com/kubernetes/dashboard/tree/master/aio/deploy
</code></pre> 
  </blockquote> 
  <h1><a href="#附录" name="附录">附录</a></h1> 
  <pre><code class="shell">kubectl delete node --all # 删除所有的节点
kubeadm reset -f # 重置kubeadm
modprobe -r ipip
lsmod
rm -rf ~/.kube/
rm -rf /etc/kubernetes/
rm -rf /etc/systemd/system/kubelet.service.d
rm -rf /etc/systemd/system/kubelet.service
rm -rf /usr/bin/kube*
rm -rf /etc/cni
rm -rf /opt/cni
rm -rf /var/lib/etcd
rm -rf /var/etcd
yum remove kube*
</code></pre>
